Talking about the hardware, the hotel is relatively new, and the bedding is very comfortable. Because it was a birthday, the room was decorated. The room we stayed in had a balcony, and it was very comfortable to enjoy the scenery. There is a children's club in B1 where you can play table tennis and billiards, as well as some other entertainment facilities that children like.
Let‚Äôs talk about the service. Starting from the command to park the car, the service is in place. After all, it is a hotel owned by Banyan Tree. There is nothing wrong with it. Mr. Xiao Han‚Äôs service is enthusiastic and proactive. He contacted us one day in advance and introduced the hotel to us when we checked in. , answer all questions, respond to all requests, like Mr. Xiao Han üëçüëçüëç
That night, I was lucky enough to participate in the hotel‚Äôs Earth Hour event. I took a lot of photos of the children, set off lights, and watched a guzheng performance. Everyone was very happyüòÑ
Let‚Äôs talk about the set meal. It includes a lunch, a small train and travel photography. If it is a single family, the price/performance ratio is very good, but when there are many people, this lunch becomes a bit embarrassing.
Let‚Äôs talk about the dishes. They include sea**** and egg soup, pan-fried meatloaf, asparagus and shrimp, and boiled lettuce. The hotel's approach and presentation are quite good, but the taste is average and needs to be improved.
The sea**** egg was well received and the best in the show. The fried meat patties were too thin and took a long time to fry. They were a little dry. The asparagus and shrimps were not completely absorbed when sizing the shrimps, so they were a little dehydrated in the end. üòÅ
However, the breakfast is well received. There are many varieties, including freshly made pancakes, fruit and meat buns, as well as noodles that Huzhou people like for breakfast, but there are no Qianzhang Bao. I personally think this is available and can reflect the characteristics of Huzhou.
Overall quite good, I recommend giving it a try!

msg:Huzhou Lucun Yueliu Hotel, a new Banyan Tree hotel, will open in 2021 and is located in the thousand-year-old village of Lucun, Huzhou.
I traveled to Huzhou during the National Day holiday and chose it because of its architectural shape and the fact that it was a Banyan Tree hotel. I was really attracted by its appearance when I first met. The cocoon-shaped lobby has become the symbol of the hotel, and the concave courtyard layout is very much like a Fujian earth building. The hotel's verandah is open and you can see the scenic area outside.
First, let‚Äôs talk about the hardware of the hotel: 1. Although the concave layout is very novel, the inner courtyard landscape is relatively simple, with only a simple waterscape and ground paving in two colors. So what is the view that guests can see from the balcony of the room? The recessed layout brings about a problem. The echo is very loud. As long as someone talks inside, it will be infinitely amplified, which often affects the rest of the night. 2. The hotel's exterior corridor is a steel structure. Although it is a renovation project, the hotel did not perform sound insulation trea**ent after taking over. As long as there are children running on it, it will be felt in the room. 3. Because it is a renovation project, the verandah faces the scenery, and only rooms on the first floor can see the outside scenery. When I asked the hotel service staff, they told me to watch the scenery from the corridor. I just wanted to ask him, You can't see the scenery from the hotel room. Who would go out of the room and stand in the corridor to see the scenery? If you look at it this way, you may go directly to the scenic area to see it. Since it is in the scenic area, if the guest room can face the scenery outside, can't it also allow guests to see the scenery? You can enjoy it while sitting in the room or lying on the bed. Traveling is for relaxation. 4. Let‚Äôs talk about the layout of the guest rooms in the hotel. There is no big problem with the overall layout, but the details are too lacking. Because it belongs to the Banyan Tree Group, my expectations are still relatively high, but I still haven‚Äôt seen any thoughtful design in the hotel. 5. Let‚Äôs talk about the selection of the faucet for the wash basin first. The faucet is very long and very close to the front of the wash basin. It was not considered at all that when the water was turned on, all the water splashed onto the countertop and water was everywhere. 6. The mirror above the wash basin is even more useless. The wash basin is not against the wall, leaving a raised countertop where things can be placed. There is nothing wrong with this design, but it can be completely disconnected at the mirror, allowing guests to get up close. I can see the mirror, and I can also see more of myself (because there is no full-length mirror in the room). I always set up a makeup mirror next to it, but after all, it can only reflect part of the picture, not the overall feeling, and the mirror on the sink is far away. It's far away and can't be seen clearly. I think all ladies can understand. 7. The faucet in the bathroom cannot be fixed. As the water volume is turned up, it rotates and sprays directly against the wall. I have only encountered this situation in express hotels, but I did not expect to encounter it in Banyan Tree hotels. 8. The place where toiletries are placed in the bathroom can only store 3 bottles of hotel stuff. The width is just right, but there is no place to put the products that the residents need to put. The hole is very high, which is completely useless. 8. The individually designed bottle shape of the hotel toiletries is considered thoughtful, but it is very difficult to press it. Even a weak woman cannot press it. The humanized design is too lacking and only the appearance is emphasized. 9. The shape and material of the door of the wardrobe at the entrance of the room are good, but the door is relatively tall and wide, and the selection of the door shaft is not careful, so it requires a lot of force to open the door. At present, the door has fallen because it is too heavy. The guide door It cannot be closed securely. Everyone knows that when the wardrobe is opened, there is a light, and when it is closed, the light goes out, but it cannot be closed securely, but light still leaks out when sleeping at night. 10. There are no bags in the closet. The Banyan Tree Hotel is actually not as good as an ordinary hotel. I tried to find a paper bag to buy things, but I couldn‚Äôt find them. The hotel logo is printed on the paper bag, which also promotes the hotel and reflects humanized service. I believe the hotel will not calculate the price of a paper bag or cloth bag. 11. Let‚Äôs talk about the hotel breakfast. I‚Äôm really looking forward to the hotel‚Äôs breakfast, because it can reflect the quality of the hotel. Overall, the variety and taste of the breakfast are good, but I still have to complain about 4 points. The first point is breakfast. The layout is a bit unreasonable. The bread is arranged separately, the fancy bread is next to the pancakes, and the toast is in the cereal area, separated by pillars, so I can't find it at all. Secondly, there is a problem with the height of the chairs in the dining area. They are 50 centimeters higher, causing guests to bend down to eat (I am not tall, only 1.62 meters). The third point is the service problem. The hotel told us that the meal would end at 10:30, but at 10:10, some of the food was gone. The service staff asked the service staff to put and unload the fruit. They were very unhappy and had a very bad attitude. They shook the plate hard in front of their face, and Some items were not replenished until 10:30. The fourth point is the dining experience. I think that if the guests stop eating at 10:30, then it should be the guests dining before 10:30, rather than the service staff quickly putting the food in their own bowls before this. 10:15 There are service staff every minute, making pancakes and cooking noodles. This feeling makes customers very uncomfortable. The hotel provides employee benefits and there is no problem in providing breakfast, but after 10:30, guests can finish getting food, so customers I have no objection, but customers are also getting food, and service staff are also getting food, for fear of running out. 12. Finally, let‚Äôs talk about the software. The overall service of the hotel is good and enthusiastic. I also listen to the opinions of customers with an open mind. I would like to make some suggestions for new employees to strengthen their service awareness. I went online at night and asked the front desk. A waiter answered the phone and didn‚Äôt know what to do. I connected and asked the service staff next to me to wait, but I went to answer another call myself. The other service staff didn‚Äôt know whether he was busy or didn‚Äôt hear me, so he just left me on the other end of the phone. After waiting for a while, no one came. Reply, I hung up the phone directly to find my account manager. Asked how to connect again, I found that there was a problem with the connection interface. It was not clear whether the input was pinyin or Chinese, and whether the input was a surname or a full name was not clearly expressed. It is recommended to set up a "how to go online" sign on the phone and give an example, so that it is convenient. Customers can go online without having to make phone calls.
Finally, I would like to explain that the overall experience of staying here is good, but because it is a Banyan Tree hotel, I came with expectations, but there are still some details, so I hope you can take a look at the hotel, and I hope the hotel will get better and better!
